Content */}\n      <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden bg-gray-50">\n        {children}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\n// Draggable Divider Component\nconst DraggableDivider: React.FC<{\n  isHorizontal: boolean;\n  onDrag: (delta: number) => void;\n  onDragEnd: () => void;\n}> = ({ isHorizontal, onDrag, onDragEnd }) => {\n  const [isDragging, setIsDragging] = useState(false);\n\n  const (e: MouseEvent) => {\n      if (!isDragging) return;\n      \n      const deltaX = e.clientX - startX;\n      const deltaY = e.clientY - startY;\n      const delta = isHorizontal ? deltaX : deltaY;\n      \n      onDrag(delta);\n    };\n    \n    const handleMouseUp = () => {\n      setIsDragging(false);\n      onDragEnd();\n      document.removeEventListener(\'mousemove\', handleMouseMove);\n };\n\n  return (\n    <div\n      className={`\n        ${isHorizontal \n          ? \'w-1 hover:w-2 cursor-col-resize\' \n          : \'h-1 hover:h-2 cursor-row-resize\'\n        }\n        ${isDragging ? \'bg-blue-500\' : \'bg-gray-300 hover:bg-blue-400\'}\n        transition-all duration-150 relative z-10\n      `}\n      onMouseDown={handleMouseDown}\n    >\n      {isDragging && (\n (onLoadLayout) {\n      const saved = onLoadLayout();\n      if (saved) {\n        setSizes(saved.sizes);\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Load from localStorage\n    const saved = localStorage.getItem(\'splitview-layout\');\n    if (saved) {\n      try {\n        const config: SplitViewConfig = JSON.parse(saved);\n        setSizes(config.sizes);\n      } catch (error) {\n        console.error(\'Failed to load layout:\', error);\n      }\n    }\n  }, [onLoadLayout]);\n\n  // Initialize layout on mount\n  useEffect(() => {\n    loadLayout();\n  }, [loadLayout]);\n\n  // Handle containerRef.current.getBoundingClientRect();\n    const containerSize = layout === \'horizontal\' ? containerRect.width : containerRect.height;\n    const deltaPercent = (delta / containerSize) * Calculate new sizes\n      newSizes[dividerIndex] = Math.max(10, Math.min(80, currentSize + deltaPercent));\n      newSizes[dividerIndex + 1] = Math.max(10, Math.min(80, nextSize - deltaPercent));\n      \n      // Normalize to ensure sum is 100\n      const total = newSizes.reduce((sum, size) => sum + size, 0);\n      if (total !== 100) {\n        const diff = (100 - total) / newSizes.length;\n        return newSizes.map(size => size + diff);\n      }\n      \n      return newSizes;\n    });\n  }, [layout]);\n\n  // Handle divider drag end\n  const handleDividerDragEnd = useCallback(() => {\n    setIsDragging(false);\n    saveLayout();\n  }, [saveLayout]);\n\n  // Panel management functions\n  const togglePin = useCallback((panelIndex: number) => {\n    setPanels(prev => prev.map((panel,     break;\n      case \'focus-left\':\n        setSizes([70, 30]);\n        break;\n      case \'focus-right\':\n        setSizes([30, 70]);\n        break;\n      case \'focus-center\':\n        setSizes([25, 50, 25]);\n        break;\n    }\n    \n    saveLayout();\n  }, [panels, saveLayout]);\n\n  // Get visible children\n  const visibleChildren = children.filter((_, index) => {child}\n                </Panel>\n              </div>\n            );\n          })}\n        </div>\n      );\n    }\n\n    if ((isHorizontal || isVertical) && visibleChildren.length > 1) {\n      // Horizontal or Vertical split layout\n      return (\n        <div className={`flex ${isVertical ? \'flex-col\' : \'flex-row\'} h-full`}>\n          {visibleChildren.map((child, index) => {\n            const originalIndex = children.indexOf(child);\n            const panel = panels[originalIndex];\n            const size = sizes[originalIndex] || 100 / visibleChildren.length;\n            \n            return (\n              <React.Fragment key={originalIndex}>\n                <div \n                  className={`relative ${isVertical ? \'\' : \'flex-shrink-0\'}`}\n DhikrItem {\n  id: string;\n  text: string;\n  translation: string;\n  count: number;\n  totalCount: number;\n  category: string;\n}\n\ninterface LocationSettings {\n  latitude: number;\n  longitude: number;\n  city: string;\n  country: string;\n  timezone: string;\n}\n\ninterface UserSettings {\n  religion: \'islam\' | \'christianity\' | \'judaism\' | \'hinduism\' | \'buddhism\' | \'none\' | 1,\n    category: \'tawhid\'\n  }\n];\n\nconst MOCK_PRAYER_TIMES = {\n  islam: {\n    fajr: { name: \'Fajr\', time: \'05:30\', icon: Sunrise },\n    dhuhr: { name: \'Dhuhr\', time: \'12:30\', icon: christianity: {\n    morning: { name: \'Morning Prayer\', time: \'07:00\', icon: Sunrise },\n    noon: { name: \'Angelus\', time: \'12:00\', icon: Sun },\n    evening: { name: \'Evening Prayer\', mincha: { name: \'Mincha\', time: \'13:00\', icon: Sun },\n    maariv: { name: \'Maariv\', time: \'19:00\', icon: Sunset }\n  }\n};\n\nconst DEFAULT_SETTINGS: UserSettings = {\n  religion: \'islam\',\n  notificationsEnabled: true,\n  soundEnabled: true,\n  prayerNotifications: true,\n  reminderNotifications: true,\n  autoAdjustForTimezone: true,\n  location: {\n    latitude: 40.7128,\n    longitude: -74.0060,\n    city: \'New York\',\n    country: \'USA\',\n    timezone: \'America/New_York\'\n  },\n  customReminders: [],\n  language: \'en\'\n};\n\n// Main Component\nexport const ReminderAndPrayerWidget: React.FC = () => {\n  const [settings, setSettings] = useState<UserSettings>(DEFAULT_SETTINGS);\n  const [currentTime, setCurrentTime] = useState(new Date());\n  const [prayerTimes, setPrayerTimes] = useState<PrayerTime[]>([]);\n  const [nextPrayer, setNextPrayer] = useState<PrayerTime | null>(null);\n  const [reminders, setReminders] = useState<Reminder[]>([]);\n  const [showSettings, setShowSettings] = useState(false);\n  const [showAddReminder, setShowAddReminder] = useState(false);\n  const [showDhikr, setShowDhikr] = useState(false);\n  const [dhikrCounts, setDhikrCounts] = useState<{ [key: string]: number }>({});\n  const [isCountingDhikr, setIsCountingDhikr] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  \n  const timeIntervalRef = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout>();\n  const notificationRef = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout>();\n\n  // Prayer times calculation (simplified - replace with real API)\n  const calculatePrayerTimes = useCallback((location: LocationSettings, date: Date) => {\n    const prayerSchedule = MOCK_PRAYER_TIMES[settings.religion] || MOCK_PRAYER_TIMES.islam;\n    const times: PrayerTime[] = [];\n    \n    Object.entries(prayerSchedule).forEach(([key, prayer]) => {\n      const [hours, minutes] = prayer.time.split(\':\').map(Number);\n      const prayerTime = new Date(date);\n      prayerTime.setHours(hours, minutes, 0, 0);\n      \n      const hasPassed = prayerTime < date;\n      \n      times.push({\n        name: prayer.name,\n        time: prayer.time,\n        nextTime: prayer.time,\n        hasPassed,\n        isNext: false\n      });\n    });\n\n    // Find next prayer\n    const nowHours = date.getHours();\n    const nowMinutes = date.getMinutes();\n    const currentTimeInMinutes = nowHours * 60 + nowMinutes;\n\n    times.forEach((prayer, index) => {\n      const [hours, minutes] = prayer.time.split(\':\').map(Number);\n      const prayerTimeInMinutes = hours * 60 + minutes;\n      \n      if (!prayer.hasPassed && (!nextPrayer || prayerTimeInMinutes < currentTimeInMinutes)) {\n        prayer.isNext = true;\n        setNextPrayer(prayer);\n      }\n    });\n\n    return times;\n  }, [settings.religion]);\n\n  // Get time until next prayer\n  const getTimeUntilPrayer = useCallback((prayerTime: string) => {\n    const [hours, minutes] = prayerTime.split(\':\').map(Number);\n    const now = currentTime;\n    const prayerDate = new Date(now);\n    prayerDate.setHours(hours, minutes, 0, 0);\n    \n    if (prayerDate <= now) {\n      prayerDate.setDate(prayerDate.getDate() + 1);\n    }\n    \n    const diff = prayerDate.getTime() - now.getTime();\n    const diffHours = Math.floor(diff / (1000 * 60 * 60));\n    const diffMinutes = Math.floor((diff % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60));\n    \n    return `${diffHours}h ${diffMinutes}m`;\n  }, [currentTime]);\n\n  // Check and trigger notifications\n  const checkNotifications = useCallback(() => {\n    if (!settings.notificationsEnabled) return;\n\n    const now = currentTime;\n    const currentHours = now.getHours();\n    const currentMinutes = now.getMinutes();\n    const currentTimeStr = `${currentHours.toString().padStart(2, \'0\')}:${currentMinutes.toString().padStart(2, \'0\')}`;\n\n    // Check prayer times\n    if (settings.prayerNotifications) {\n      prayerTimes.forEach(prayer => {\n        if (prayer.time === currentTimeStr && !prayer.hasPassed) {\n          // Trigger prayer notification\n          if (settings.soundEnabled) {\n            playNotificationSound(\'prayer\');\n          }\n          showNotification(`${prayer.name} Time`, `It\'s time for ${prayer.name} prayer`);\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    // Check reminders\n    if (settings.reminderNotifications) {\n      reminders.forEach(reminder => {\n        if (reminder.isActive && reminder.time === currentTimeStr) {\n          const today = now.toLocaleDateString(\'en-US\', { weekday: \'long\' }).toLowerCase();\n          const dayMap: { [key: string]: string } = {\n            \'monday\': \'mon\', \'tuesday\': \'tue\', \'wednesday\': \'wed\',\n            \'thursday\': \'thu\', \'friday\': \'fri\', \'saturday\': \'sat\', \'sunday\': \'sun\'\n          };\n          \n          if (reminder.days.includes(dayMap[today]) || reminder.days.includes(\'all\')) {\n            if (settings.soundEnabled) {\n              playNotificationSound(\'reminder\');\n            }\n            showNotification(reminder.title, reminder.description);\n          }\n        }\n      });\n    }\n  }, [currentTime, settings, prayerTimes, reminders]);\n\n  // Play notification sound (mock implementation)\n  const playNotificationSound = useCallback((type: \'prayer\' | \'reminder\') => {\n    const audio = new Audio();\n    audio.volume = settings.soundEnabled ? 0.5 : 0;\n    \n    // Mock sound files - replace with actual audio files\n    if (type === \'prayer\') {\n      audio.src = \'/sounds/adhan.mp3\';\n    } else {\n      audio.src = \'/sounds/reminder.mp3\';\n    }\n    \n    audio.play().catch(console.error);\n  }, [settings.soundEnabled]);\n\n  // Show browser notification\n  const showNotification = useCallback((title: string, body: string) => {\n    if (\'Notification\' in window && Notification.permission === \'granted\') {\n      new Notification(title, {\n        body,\n        icon: \'/icons/prayer-icon.png\',\n        badge: \'/icons/badge.png\'\n      });\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Dhikr counter functions\n  const incrementDhikrCount = useCallback((dhikrId: string) => {\n    setDhikrCounts(prev => {\n      const current = prev[dhikrId] || 0;\n      const dhikr = MOCK_DHIKR_ITEMS.find(item => item.id === dhikrId);\n      \n      if (dhikr && current < dhikr.totalCount) {\n        return { ...prev, [dhikrId]: current + 1 };\n      }\n      \n      return prev;\n    });\n  }, []);\n\n  const resetDhikrCount = useCallback((dhikrId: const stopDhikrCounting = useCallback(() => {\n    setIsCountingDhikr(null);\n  }, []);\n\n  // Add new reminder\n  const addReminder = useCallback((reminder: Omit<Reminder, \'id\' | \'createdAt\'>) reminder.id === reminderId \n        ? { ...reminder, isActive: !reminder.isActive }\n        : reminder\n    ));\n  }, []);\n\n  // Delete reminder\n  const deleteReminder = useCallback((reminderId: && Notification.permission === \'default\') {\n      Notification.requestPermission();\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Update current time\n  useEffect(() => {\n    timeIntervalRef.current = setInterval(() => {\n      setCurrentTime(new Date());\n    }, 1000);\n\n    return () => {\n      if (timeIntervalRef.current) {\n        clearInterval(timeIntervalRef.current);\n      }\n    };\n  }, []);\n\n  // Update prayer times\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const times = calculatePrayerTimes(settings.location, currentTime);\n    setPrayerTimes(times);\n  }, [currentTime, settings.location, return () => {\n      if (notificationRef.current) {\n        clearInterval(notificationRef.current);\n      }\n    };\n  }, [checkNotifications]);\n\n  // Initialize dhikr counts\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const initialCounts: { [key: string]: number } = {};\n    MOCK_DHIKR_ITEMS.forEach(item => {\n      initialCounts[item.id] = 0;\n    });\n    setDhikrCounts(initialCounts);\n  }, []);\n\n  // {currentTime.toLocaleTimeString()}\n            </div>\n          </div>\n          \n          <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">\n            <button\n              onClick={() =>     onClick={() => setShowAddReminder(!showAddReminder)}\n              className="p-2 text-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-100 rounded-lg"\n              title="Add reminder"\n            >\n              <Plus className="w-4 h-4" />\n            </button>\n            <button\n              onClick={() => setShowSettings(!showSettings)}\n              className="p-2 text-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-100     <AddReminderForm onSave={addReminder} onCancel={() => setShowAddReminder(false)} />\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Dhikr Counter */}\n      {showDhikr && (\n        <div {MOCK_DHIKR_ITEMS.map((dhikr) => {\n              const count = dhikrCounts[dhikr.id] || 0;\n              const isActive = isCountingDhikr === dhikr.id;\n              const isComplete = count >= dhikr.totalCount;\n              \n              return (\n                <div key={dhikr.id} className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 bg-white rounded-lg">\n                  <div className="flex-1">\n                    <div className="font-medium text-gray-900">{dhikr.text}</div>\n                    <div className="text-sm text-gray-600">{dhikr.translation}</div>\n        </div>\n                      <div className="flex-1 bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2">\n                        <div \n                          className={`h-2 rounded-full transition-all ${\n                            isComplete ? \'bg-green-500\' : \'bg-blue-500\'\n                          }`}\n                          style={{ width: `${(count / dhikr.totalCount) * 100}%` }}\n                 </button>\n                    )}\n                    \n                    <button\n                      onClick={() => resetDhikrCount(dhikr.id)}\n </button>\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n              );\n            })}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      )}\n\n      {/* Main Content */}\n      <div className="flex-1     <VolumeX className="w-3 h-3 text-gray-400" />\n                <span>Notifications disabled</span>\n              </>\n            )}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n};\n\n// Add Reminder Form Component\nconst AddReminderForm: React.FC<{\n  onSave: (reminder: Omit<Reminder, \'id\' | \'createdAt\'>) => void;\n  onCancel: () => void;\n}> = ({ onSave, onCancel }) => {\n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({\n    title: \'\',\n    description: \'\',\n    time: \'12:00\',\n    days: [\'mon\', \'tue\', \'wed\', \'thu\', \'fri\'],\n    category: \'general\' as const,\n    religion: \'islam\' as const,\n    soundEnabled: true,\n    recurring: true\n  });\n\n  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    onSave(formData);\n  };\n\n  const toggleDay = (day: string) => {\n    setFormData(prev => ({\n      ...prev,\n      days: prev.days.includes(day) \n        ? prev.days.filter(d => d !== day)\n        : [...prev.days, day]\n    }));\n  };\n\n  const days = [\n    { value: \'mon\', label: \'Mon\' },\n    { value: \'tue\', label: \'Tue\' },\n    { value: \'wed\', label: \'Wed\' },\n    { value: \'thu\', label: \'Thu\' },\n    { value: \'fri\', label: \'Fri\' },\n    { value: \'sat\', label: \'Sat\' },\n    { value: \'sun\', label: \'Sun\' }\n  ];\n\n  return (\n    <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-3">\n      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">\n        <div>\n          <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">\n            Title\n          </label>\n          <input\n            type="text"\n            value={formData.title}\n            onChange={(e) => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, title: e.target.value }))}\n               async with session.get(url, proxy=proxy) as response:\n                    if response.status == 200:\n                        html = await response.text()\n                        return self.parse_product_page(html, url)\n                    else:\n                        logger.warning(f"HTTP {response.status} for {url}")\n                        if proxy:\n                            self.proxy_manager.mark_proxy_failed(proxy)\n                        return None\n                        \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Error scraping {url}:       \'.current-price\',\n            \'.product-price\',\n            \'[data-testid="price"]\',\n            \'.price-current\',\n            \'.sale-price\',\n            \'.amount\'\n        ]\n        \n        for selector in price_selectors:\n            element = soup.select_one(selector)\n            if element:\n                price_text = element.get_text(strip=True)\n """Parse price text to float"""\n        # Remove currency symbols and whitespace\n        price_text = re.sub(r\'[^\\d.,]\', \'\', price_text)\n        \n        # Handle different decimal separators\n        if \',\' in price_text and \'.\' in price_text:\n            # Assume format like 1,234.56\n            price_text = price_text.replace(\',\', \'\')\n        elif \',\' in price_text:\n            # Could be 1,234 or 1.234 (depending on locale)\n            parts = price_text.split(\',\')\n            if len(parts) == 2 and len(parts[1]) <= 2:\n                # Likely decimal separator (e.g., 123,45)\n                price_text = price_text.replace(\',\', \'.\')\n            else:\n                # Likely thousand separator\n                price_text = price_text.replace(\',\', \'\')\n        \n        try:\n            return float(price_text)\n        except ValueError:\n            return 0.0\n    \n    def extract_description(self, soup: BeautifulSoup) -> str:\n        """Extract product description"""\n        desc_selectors = [\n            \'.product-description\',\n            \'.description\',\n            \'[data-testid="product-description"]\',\n            \'.product-details\',\n            \'.details\',\n            \'.product-content\',\n            \'meta[name="description"]\'\n        ]\n        \n        for selector in desc_selectors:\n            if selector.startswith(\'meta\'):\n                element = soup.select_one(selector)\n                if element and element.get(\'content\'):\n                    return element.get(\'content\')\n            else:\n                element = soup.select_one(selector)\n                if element:\n                    desc = element.get_text(strip=True)\n                    if len(desc) > 20:\n                        return desc\n        \n        return ""\n    \n    def extract_availability(self, soup: \'[data-testid="availability"]\',\n            \'.in-stock\',\n            \'.out-of-stock\'\n        ]\n        \n        for selector in availability_selectors:\n            element = availability:\n                    return \'out_of_stock\'\n                elif \'in stock\' in availability or \'available\' in availability:\n                    return \'in_stock\'\n                elif \'limited\' in availability:\n                    return \'limited\'\n        \n        return \'unknown\'\n    \n    def extract_rating(self, soup: BeautifulSoup) -> Optional[float]:\n        """Extract product rating"""\n        rating_selectors = [\n            \'.rating\',\n            \'.stars\',\n            \'[data-testid="rating"]\',\n            \'.review-rating\',\n            \'.average-rating\'\n        ]\n        \n        for selector in rating_selectors:\n            element = soup.select_one(selector)\n            if element:\n                rating_text = element.get_text(strip=True)\n                rating = self.parse_rating(rating_text)\n                if rating is not None:\n                    return rating\n        \n        return None\n    \n    def parse_rating(self, rating_text: str) -> Optional[float]:\n        """Parse rating text to float"""\n        # Look for patterns like "4.5", "4.5 out of 5", "4.5/5"\n        patterns = [\n            r\'(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*out\\s*of\\s*5\',\n            r\'(\\d+\\.?\\d*)/5\',\n            r\'(\\d+\\.?\\d*)\\s*stars?\',\n            r\'^(\\d+\\.?\\d*)$\'\n        ]\n        \n        for pattern in patterns:\n            match = re.search(pattern, rating_text, re.IGNORECASE)\n            if match:\n                try:\n                    rating = float(match.group(1))\n                    if 0 <= rating <= 5:\n                        return rating\n                except ValueError:\n                    continue\n        \n        return None\n    \n    def extract_reviews_count(self, \'[data-testid="reviews-count"]\',\n            \'.num-reviews\',\n            \'.reviews\'\n        ]\n        \n        for selector in reviews_selectors:\n            element = not None:\n                    return count\n        \n        return None\n    \n    def parse_number(self, text: str) -> Optional[int]:\n        """Parse number from text"""\n        # Remove non-digit characters except for k, m, etc.\n        text = re.sub(r\'[^\\dkm.,]\', \'\', text.lower())\n        \n        # Handle k (thousands) and m (millions)\n        multiplier = 1\n        if \'k\' in text:\n            multiplier = 1000\n            text = text.replace(\'k\', \'\')\n        elif \'m\' in text:\n            multiplier = 1000000\n            text = text.replace(\'m\', \'\')\n        \n        text = text.replace(\',\', \'\')\n        \n        try:\n            return int(float(text) * multiplier)\n        except ValueError:\n            return None\n    \n    def extract_images(self, soup: BeautifulSoup, base_url: str) -> List[str]:\n        """Extract product images"""\n        images = []\n        \n        # Look for product images\n        img_selectors = parse_date(self, date_text: str) -> Optional[datetime]:\n        """Parse date from text"""\n        # Common date formats\n        formats = [\n            \'%Y-%m-%d\',\n            \'%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S\',\n            \'%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ\',\n            \'%d/%m/%Y\',\n            \'%m/%d/%Y\',\n            \'%d-%m-%Y\',\n            \'%m-%d-%Y\'\n        ]\n        \n        for def extract_specifications(self, soup: BeautifulSoup) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Extract product specifications"""\n        specs = {}\n        \n        # Look for specification tables or lists\n        spec_selectors = [\n            \'.specifications table\',\n            \'.specs table\',\n            \'.product-details table\',\n            \'.technical-specs table\',\n            \'.specs-list\'\n        ]\n        \n        for selector in spec_selectors:\n            element = soup.select_one(selector)\n            if element:\n                rows = element.select(\'tr\')      return await self.scrape_product_page(url)\n        \n        # Execute scraping tasks\n        tasks = [scrape_with_semaphore(url) for url in urls]\n        \n        for i, task in
